          <h1>
           <span class="color-black">
            THE PHILLIPS LYTLE WAY:
           </span>
           <span class="color-copper">
            SERVICE ABOVE
           </span>
           ALL.
          </h1>
          <p>
           The highest level of service isn’t just something we preach at Phillips Lytle, it’s what we practice each and every day. It’s our passion to deliver, guided by a pragmatism that ensures calculated, sound decisions aimed at our clients’ business goals.
          </p>
